make[1]: Entering directory '/tmp/libinfinity/src/libinfinity-0.6.4/po'
mkdir -p /tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity/usr/share; \
catalogs='ca.gmo de.gmo'; \
for cat in $catalogs; do \
  cat=`basename $cat`; \
  case "$cat" in \
    *.gmo) destdir=/usr/share/locale;; \
    *)     destdir=/usr/lib/locale;; \
  esac; \
  lang=`echo $cat | sed 's/\.gmo$//'`; \
  dir=/tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity$destdir/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  mkdir -p $dir; \
  if test -r $cat; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $cat $dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo; \
    echo "installing $cat as $dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$cat $dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$cat as" \
	 "$dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $cat.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $cat.m $dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $cat.m as $dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$cat.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$cat.m \
	$dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$cat as" \
	   "$dir/libinfinity-0.6.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
installing ca.gmo as /tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity/usr/share/locale/ca/LC_MESSAGES/libinfinity-0.6.mo
installing de.gmo as /tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity/usr/share/locale/de/LC_MESSAGES/libinfinity-0.6.mo
if test "libinfinity" = "glib"; then \
  mkdir -p /tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity/usr/share/glib-2.0/gettext/po; \
  /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./Makefile.in.in \
		  /tmp/libinfinity/pkg/libinfinity/usr/share/glib-2.0/gettext/po/Makefile.in.in; \
else \
  : ; \
fi
